Location and transportation: 
Along Chang'an Avenue, in the Xidan business district, the status strength can be imagined 

Room view: 
The executive room is high-end! Although the window can't be opened and the glass is a bit blurry, the view is good! The layout of the small suite is quite good inside~ I like the bed, very comfortable~ 

Parking:

The front desk brother Shuo Shuo is very enthusiastic! The service is very thoughtful~ I like to order takeout, and he also asked the courier to put it in the robot and deliver it upstairs

name:P‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äço
info:Family Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 4, 2023
msg:It is located less than a 5-minute walk from China's Xinan Station and about 5 minutes from Xiamen Station, and is located in the Joy City shopping mall. Major tourist attractions such as Tiananmen, Forbidden City, and Wangfujing can be reached at once by taking Line 1, and since it is located in the center, transportation is very convenient. The room was very clean, there was no cigarette smell at all and all facilities were in like new condition. Even though I visited during the National Day holiday, the Xidan area was not very crowded and was pleasant. Breakfast is available for 100 yuan per person, and most of the menu is Chinese, so please keep this in mind. Overall, I was very satisfied with everything, but was disappointed by the lack of English-speaking staff. It boasts an excellent location with all amenities nearby, and is quieter than other tourist attractions, so I would like to visit this place again the next time I visit Beijing. The staff were very friendly, and most of all, I really liked the condition of the accommodation. For Korean travelers, you can purchase and receive a refund for an Ikatong (transportation card) at Sidan Station, so it would be convenient to purchase a card here and travel. I paid for my accommodation with Alipay and had no problems using my international card. Highly recommended!

name:A‚Äçn‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçy‚Äçm‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted July 15, 2023
msg:Say it first:
The location is unbeatable. It is in the center of Xidan. All scenic spots are basically accessible by subway. It is not too far away. Not far from the door is the subway entrance of Line 1 and Line 4. The hotel is connected to the 6th floor of the shopping mall, which is particularly convenient for personal travel or taking children to eat, drink and have fun. The hotel staff are quite enthusiastic and will take the initiative to say hello.
The room was fairly neat and clean, and there was no dust accumulated in any of the corners. The room is designed in a simple style, which I quite like.
After applying over the phone, I agreed to delay the check-out time until 3 o'clock, which was not easy during the peak summer season.
What can be improved:
The lobby is really too basic, and the elevator design is hard to describe. My first impression when I walked in was that I wanted to retreat.
I booked a family room, but there was no partition in the bathroom and it had a single basin, which was really inconvenient for parents traveling with children.
The lighting design of the room is too simple and not warm and comfortable enough. The curtains are not electric and inconvenient. Some of the small items in the room are not refined and high-end enough.
The water in the shower room is relatively small and the bath is not comfortable enough. The room is not equipped with a bathtub. Although I don't use a bathtub, I am used to washing my hair in the morning. I usually use the shower head of the bathtub to wash my hair outside, which is inconvenient. Not equipped with a bathtub, which is still rare in a hotel with a price of 1200.
Summary: For those who have high location requirements and care about convenient travel, eating, drinking and entertainment, the Joy Hotel will still meet their needs. But for those who have high requirements for room comfort, there may be better options. But in terms of overall evaluation, we booked early, and the family room cost 1,200, with two 1.5 large beds, and the price/performance ratio was still appropriate.
